style="color: #000000;">Ruger</font></h2> <h2><font style="color: #000000;"><span>SR1911 .45 ACP 4.25" Barrel Low Glare Stainless Steel Finish Two 7-round magazines<br></span></font></h2> <p><font face="book antiqua,palatino" size="3"><span>Original 1911 Series 70 design. Hardwood grips and checkered backstrap. CNC machined. Stainless steel barrel and bushing are produced from the same bar stock on the same machine for improved accuracy. Positive barrel lock-up. Oversized ejection port and extended magazine release. Lightweight aluminum skeletonized trigger features an adjustable over-travel stop. Dovetailed 3-dot sight system features a Novak LoMount Carry rear and standard front sight. Includes titanium firing pin, 7-round magazine, bushing wrench and soft case.</span></font></p> <p><font face="book antiqua,palatino" size="3"><span><img src="../../../../Data/Default/Images/uploads/ruger/ruger-6702-736676067022-1.jpg" alt="" width="540" height="381"><img src="../../../../Data/Default/Images/uploads/ruger/ruger-6702-736676067022-2.jpg" alt="" width="540" height="380"><img src="../../../../Data/Default/Images/uploads/ruger/ruger-6702-736676067022-3.jpg" alt="" width="540" height="421"><img src="../../../../Data/Default/Images/uploads/ruger/ruger-6702-736676067022-4.jpg" alt="" width="540" height="344"><br></span></font></p></span></div> </div><div id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_uxProductTabs_ProductTabs_TabSpecifications" class="ajax__tab_panel" style="display:none;visibility:hidden;"> <div class="Features"> <span id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_uxProductTabs_ProductTabs_TabSpecifications_ProductsSpecifications"><ul><li>Category : Pistols</li><li>Type : Pistol</li><li>Action : Single</li><li>Caliber : 45 Automatic Colt Pistol (ACP)</li><li>Barrel Length : 4.3"</li><li>Capacity : 8+1</li><li>Safety : Manual Thumb/Grip</li><li>Grips : Wood</li><li>Sights : Novak Fixed 3-Dot</li><li>Weight : 36 oz</li><li>Frame Finish : Stainless</li></ul></span></div> </div><div id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_uxProductTabs_ProductTabs_pnlCustomerReviews" class="ajax__tab_panel" style="display:none;visibility:hidden;"> <div class="Reviews"> <div id="Review"> <div id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_uxProductTabs_ProductTabs_pnlCustomerReviews_uxProductReviews_UpdatePnlProductReviewDetails"> <div class="Sorting"> <span class="TitleStyle"> Reviewed by <span id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_uxProductTabs_ProductTabs_pnlCustomerReviews_uxProductReviews_CustomersCnt">12</span> customer </span>&nbsp; Not only is it a work of art, and I commend the Ruger gunsmiths for the quality it their trade, but it performs better than any 1911 I have shot right out of the box. I took this 1911 and cleaned it, with no other adjustments right to the range. It ate up every kind of ammo I had with me, including my lead ball reloads, and not one misfire or jamb. It grouped like it had been broke it, and accurized. With every 1911 I have had before, I have had a problem with them feeding the tapered bullets of the hollow point defense loads. They want to feed only round ball, especially the Colts. I have owned a Colt that would feed anything, but round ball ammo. I have to polish the feeding ramp to get them to feed all kinds of ammo. With this Ruger, I don't have to do anything to it. Why pay thousands of dollars for name brand 1911's, when you can get the best in this Ruger ...? This is another example Ruger continues to put out a quality made firearm at a reasonable price.</div> <div class="Row"> By <span class="Text"> Old Man</span> from <span class="Text"> Boise, Idaho</span></div> </div> </div> </td> </tr><tr> <td class="ReviewItem"> <div class="ItemStyle"> <div class="Title"> <span class="Subject"> Reflective of Ruger's Made in the USA Quality</span>, October 06, 2015</div> <div class="Content"> <div class="StarRating"> <img src="/themes/New5/Images/Star.gif" valign="absmiddle" alt="" border="0"><img src="/themes/New5/Images/Star.gif" valign="absmiddle" alt="" border="0"><img src="/themes/New5/Images/Star.gif" valign="absmiddle" alt="" border="0"><img src="/themes/New5/Images/Star.gif" valign="absmiddle" alt="" border="0"><img src="/themes/New5/Images/Star.gif" valign="absmiddle" alt="" border="0"></div> <div class="Row"> I have owned several 1911s and this Ruger Commander is by far the best ! I have owned many 1911 guns in the last 5 decades, including my GI issued 1911. I also competed with a 1911 so I am familiar with them from the basic to the tricked out models. For home defense and range fun, you cannot beat the CMD. Can you carry it? Yep you can but it is not for everybody. You can get the new aluminum version for a lot more but a Glock 30 holds more rounds and is less weight so that is what I carry when I want a .45 on my hip. For me the commander length is perfect. I find 4" barrel guns balance well for me and are quick on targert without losing much.
